[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While fuzzing the function that processes path arguments for `systemctl` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`systemctl_parse_argv` → `parse_path_argument`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, AddressSanitizer flagged an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempted double‐free of a small buffer. The harness drives inputs through [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, invoking the argument parser repeatedly. On certain [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs, the code frees an allocated string inside `parse_path_argument`, and then [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fuzzing harness’s static cleanup logic frees it again.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Memory corruption: double‐free [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma form of unsafe memory deallocation that can [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlead to crashes or, in some contexts, arbitrary code execution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The first free occurs in `parse_path_argument` [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msrc/shared/parse-argument.[0m[1;92mc:68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The same pointer is freed a second time in the harness’s static destructor [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`static-destruct.h`, invoked from `fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.[0m[1;92mc:74[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The buffer in question is originally allocated or resized via `realloc` inside[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_extend_internal` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/basic/path-util.[0m[1;92mc:585[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, called from [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/basic/path-util.[0m[1;92mc:92[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The double‐free triggers an AddressSanitizer abort with a “SCARINESS: [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m” [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrating, indicating a serious memory safety violation.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/shared/parse-argument.c`, function `parse_path_argument` — manages [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation and deallocation of path strings.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/basic/path-util.c`, functions `path_extend_internal` and [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd` — handle buffer growth and absolute path computation.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/systemctl/systemctl.c`, function `systemctl_parse_argv` — orchestrates [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39margument parsing, including calls into `parse_path_argument`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c` and `static-destruct.h` — the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing harness, particularly its cleanup logic that frees resources across test [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA holistic review should focus on the lifecycle of heap‐allocated buffers in path [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing, ensuring each allocation has a single corresponding free and that static [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup in the harness does not overlap with in‐code deallocations.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msrc/shared/parse-argument.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. In the initial trace, `parse_path_argument` frees a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer when the input path is empty, and later `static_destruct` frees it again at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe end of the fuzzer callback, leading to a double-free. A patch was applied to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremove the `free` call inside the `[0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` branch, leaving only `return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen the path is empty. After rebuilding and rerunning the fuzzer, ASan still [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreports a double-free in `parse_path_argument`, now at a different line [0m[1;39m([0m[1;92m79:16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating the issue was not fully resolved by the patch.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer executes `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mfuzz-systemctl-parse-argv[0m[39m` with a one-byte testcase. [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations:  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `parse_path_argument` frees its input buffer on an empty `path` and returns.  [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In src/shared/parse-argument.c, the branch handling an empty path was simplified.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOriginal code:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          *arg = [0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  was replaced with:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allocation remains from the same path-utility routines. The double-free now [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs in a different location inside `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m79[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m after [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd` is called, indicating that there is at least one other [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruns.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone of those frees by [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m skipping the free when `path` is empty, [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only calling [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The backtrace shows:  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `parse_path_argument` frees the buffer at address `[0m[1;36m0x502000007310[0m[39m`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Later, during `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` teardown, `static_destruct` calls [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the same pointer again.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The region was originally allocated by `path_make_absolute_cwd` via `realloc`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `src/shared/parse-argument.c`, the free logic in `parse_path_argument` was [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Removed the call to free `*arg` when `[0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is true.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. After calling `[0m[1;35mpath_simplify[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, if `suppress_root && [0m[1;35mempty_or_root[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree the new buffer `p`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Added a check: if `p == *arg`, return immediately without calling [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Otherwise, call `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to free the old buffer and set [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`*arg = p`.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The goal was to avoid freeing the original buffer when `path_make_absolute_cwd` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturned it in place.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mResult after patch  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After rebuilding and rerunning with [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m iterations, the same double-free is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported, now at line [0m[1;36m83[0m[39m of `parse-argument.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe new location of the free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m parse_path_argument [0m[33m...[0m[35m/src/shared/[0m[95mparse-argument.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m83:12[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m static_destruct [0m[33m...[0m[35m/src/basic/[0m[95mstatic-destruct.h[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m95:25[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The sanitizer log confirms:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The pointer is still freed inside `parse_path_argument`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • It is freed again in `static_destruct`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The initial allocation remains from `path_make_absolute_cwd` via `realloc`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for further investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The interaction between `parse_path_argument`’s free logic and the static [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mteardown [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`static_destruct`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • How and when `static_destruct` is scheduled to free `*arg`.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Whether `parse_path_argument` should defer ownership of `*arg` to the caller.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The behavior of `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Does it always free the old buffer?  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Under what conditions does it leave the old pointer intact?  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code paths in `systemctl_parse_argv` that call `parse_path_argument`:  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Confirm that the same pointer is not freed an extra time further up.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The logic in `path_make_absolute_cwd` and `path_extend_internal`:  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Whether they sometimes return the same pointer as input.  [0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • How it manages lifetime of allocated buffers within each iteration.  [0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer-guided fuzz test of `systemctl_parse_argv` revealed a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free in `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `src/shared/parse-argument.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitial bug report showed that under certain inputs, `parse_path_argument` frees [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same pointer twice: once after path simplification and again when the fuzzer’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic destructor runs. A candidate patch removed one of the unconditional frees in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `[0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` branch and added checks to avoid freeing when the simplified [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`p`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is the same as the original argument or when suppressing root [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths. When rerunning the fuzzer with the patch applied, the sanitizer still [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreports a double-free in `parse_path_argument`, now at a different line, indicating[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat the attempt did not fully eliminate the overlapping frees.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Fuzzer run of `fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv` with AddressSanitizer triggered a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free in `parse_path_argument` at line [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m of `src/shared/parse-argument.c`.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The log shows two frees of the same [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-byte allocation at address [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x502000007310[0m[39m`:  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – First free in `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe patched function[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – Second free in the harness’s `static_destruct` after `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The allocation originated from `realloc` in `path_extend_internal` → [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd` → `parse_path_argument`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe proposed patch modifies `parse_path_argument` as follows:  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. In the `[0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` case, remove the call that frees `*arg`, simply return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. After path simplification, if `suppress_root && [0m[1;35mempty_or_root[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, only free `p`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen it differs from the original `*arg`, then return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. If `p` equals the original `*arg`, return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m immediately to avoid calling [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`free_and_replace`.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Otherwise, proceed with `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSpecifically, the diff around lines [0m[1;36m65[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m r = [0m[1;35mpath_make_absolute_cwd[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath, &p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;35mpath_simplify[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msuppress_root && [0m[1;35mempty_or_root[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mp != *arg[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         p = [0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mp == *arg[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m return [0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mResult after patch  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Fuzzer re-execution still reports a double-free in `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnow at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m85[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The sanitizer trace again shows the same allocation being freed once in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_path_argument` and once in the fuzzer harness’s `static_destruct`.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The allocation and free sites are identical in origin [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and destructor context, confirming the patch did not [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcover all free paths.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for further investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The control flow in `parse_path_argument` around all return paths—ensure no code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath frees or replaces `*arg` inadvertently before the fuzzer’s static destructor. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The semantics of `mfree`, `free_and_replace`, and their interaction with `*arg`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The harness’s `static_destruct` logic in `fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c` to see [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen and how it frees `*arg`.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The conditions under which `suppress_root` and `empty_or_root` trigger frees, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand whether they overlap with calls to `free_and_replace`.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The entire lifecycle of the buffer pointed to by `*arg` within one [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` invocation to track every allocation and deallocation.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer report generated by a libFuzzer-based test identified a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free in the function `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/shared/parse-argument.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The initial issue log shows two frees of the same [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory region: once inside `parse_path_argument` and once later during the static [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mteardown of the fuzzer harness. A patch was proposed that restructures the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mearly-exit and free logic in `parse_path_argument`, adding checks on whether the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew path buffer `p` equals the input buffer or should be suppressed. After applying[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe patch, the fuzzer run still triggers a double-free at `parse_path_argument`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow on a different line number but on the same buffer, indicating that the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempted fix did not eliminate the duplicate free.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A fuzzing run with AddressSanitizer on `fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv` called into [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_path_argument`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The sanitizer report shows:  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • An initial `realloc`-based allocation of a path buffer inside [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A call to `free` in `parse_path_argument` which is intended to replace the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal argument with an absolute path.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A second `free` of the same pointer later in the fuzzer harness’s [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`static_destruct` call.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack traces pin the bug to `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m originally[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m freeing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`*arg` and then the same memory being freed again during static teardown.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changes in `parse_path_argument` around the early return and free logic:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Remove the call `*arg = [0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on empty input and simply return.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • After computing the absolute path into `p`, skip any free-and-replace if `p == [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*arg`.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • When `suppress_root` is set and `p` is root or empty, free `p` but do not free [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe original `*arg`.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • In all other cases, call `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to swap buffers.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patched code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m64[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m90[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m looks like:  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```c[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  r = [0m[1;35mpath_make_absolute_cwd[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath, &p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mr < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;35mpath_simplify[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msuppress_root && [0m[1;35mempty_or_root[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      p = [0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPost-Patch Result  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A new fuzzing run still triggers an AddressSanitizer double-free in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_path_argument`, now reported at the patched location [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m85[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The same memory region is freed first by the patched `parse_path_argument` code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand then again by `static_destruct` in the fuzzer harness.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The log structure and offending addresses mirror the original report, confirming [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat the patch did not prevent the duplicate free.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The interaction between `parse_path_argument`’s free logic and the fuzzer harness[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mteardown [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`static_destruct`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: how ownership of the buffer is tracked and when it [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould or should not be freed.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The semantics of `free_and_replace` versus direct calls to `free` or `mfree`, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhether replacing the pointer into `*arg` leads to double-free if the original [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer is still registered for destruction.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `suppress_root` branch and the condition `p == *arg`: ensure that no [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munintended path through the function leaves the buffer in an inconsistent freed [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The lifecycle of the argument buffer allocated before entering [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_path_argument`, including any initializations or registrations for cleanup [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat happen outside this function.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overall memory management conventions in the parse-argument code, especially [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maround absolute-path construction [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`path_make_absolute_cwd`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and simplification [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`path_simplify`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, to determine correct ownership transfer.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
